\DoxyCodeLine{703 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{704 }
\DoxyCodeLine{705 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Helper function to calculate a circle's segment count given its radius and a "{}maximum error"{} value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{706 \textcolor{comment}{// Estimation of number of circle segment based on error is derived using method described in https://stackoverflow.com/a/2244088/15194693}}
\DoxyCodeLine{707 \textcolor{comment}{// Number of segments (N) is calculated using equation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{708 \textcolor{comment}{//   N = ceil ( pi / acos(1 -\/ error / r) )     where r > 0, error <= r}}
\DoxyCodeLine{709 \textcolor{comment}{// Our equation is significantly simpler that one in the post thanks for choosing segment that is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{710 \textcolor{comment}{// perpendicular to X axis. Follow steps in the article from this starting condition and you will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{711 \textcolor{comment}{// will get this result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{712 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{713 \textcolor{comment}{// Rendering circles with an odd number of segments, while mathematically correct will produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{714 \textcolor{comment}{// asymmetrical results on the raster grid. Therefore we're rounding N to next even number (7-\/>8, 8-\/>8, 9-\/>10 etc.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{715 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN(\_V)                                  ((((\_V) + 1) / 2) * 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{716 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN                     4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{717 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX                     512}}
\DoxyCodeLine{718 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC(\_RAD,\_MAXERROR)    ImClamp(IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN((int)ImCeil(IM\_PI / ImAcos(1 -\/ ImMin((\_MAXERROR), (\_RAD)) / (\_RAD)))), IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN, IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{719 }
\DoxyCodeLine{720 \textcolor{comment}{// Raw equation from IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC rewritten for 'r' and 'error'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{721 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_R(\_N,\_MAXERROR)    ((\_MAXERROR) / (1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{722 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_ERROR(\_N,\_RAD)     ((1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))) / (\_RAD))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{723 }
\DoxyCodeLine{724 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Lookup table size for adaptive arc drawing, cover full circle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{725 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{726 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE                          48 }\textcolor{comment}{// Number of samples in lookup table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{727 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{728 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_SAMPLE\_MAX                          IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE }\textcolor{comment}{// Sample index \_PathArcToFastEx() for 360 angle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{729 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2971     \textcolor{comment}{// Docking -\/ Builder function needs to be generally called before the node is used/submitted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2972     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The DockBuilderXXX functions are designed to \_eventually\_ become a public API, but it is too early to expose it and guarantee stability.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2973     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Do not hold on ImGuiDockNode* pointers! They may be invalidated by any split/merge/remove operation and every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2974     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To create a DockSpace() node, make sure to set the ImGuiDockNodeFlags\_DockSpace flag when calling DockBuilderAddNode().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2975     \textcolor{comment}{//   You can create dockspace nodes (attached to a window) \_or\_ floating nodes (carry its own window) with this API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2976     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ DockBuilderSplitNode() create 2 child nodes within 1 node. The initial node becomes a parent node.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2977     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you intend to split the node immediately after creation using DockBuilderSplitNode(), make sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2978     \textcolor{comment}{//   to call DockBuilderSetNodeSize() beforehand. If you don't, the resulting split sizes may not be reliable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2979     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Call DockBuilderFinish() after you are done.}}
